y(t) = A * sin(ωt + φ) + C

- A is the amplitude

- φ is the phase shift
- C is the vertical shift

y(t) = A * sin(ωt + φ) + C = A * sin(ωt) * cos(φ) + A * cos(ωt) * sin(φ) + C
